$('#gnn_normal').html(normal);
$('.BA-ctag1now').filter('[id^="gnn_"]').attr('className','');
$('#gnn_'+who).attr('className','BA-ctag1now');
if( 'show' != who && 1 == gnnshowing ){
$('#gnn_show').attr('className','show');
}
gnnwho = who;
gnnwhoflag = setTimeout(function(){ gnnwhoc=1; }, 200);
}

};

function guildShowIni(){
var guildBlockAry = ["push","hot","pushguild","hotwiki"];
var guildBlockIniKey = Math.floor( Math.random() * guildBlockAry.length );
guildBlockIniKey = (4 <= guildBlockIniKey || 0 >= guildBlockIniKey ) ? 0 : guildBlockIniKey;
guildShowBlock(guildBlockAry[guildBlockIniKey]);
}

function   acg_changea(who){
var list = acglist;
var listtitle = {"TV":{"r1":"平台","r3":"發售"},"AC":{"r1":"類別","r3":"發售"},"QA":{"r1":"類別","r3":"週期"}};
var ref = {"PC":{"link":"0000171","more":"0000172"},"TV":{"link":"0000173","more":"0000174"},"AC":{"link":"0000175","more":"0000176"},"QA":{"link":"0000183","more":"0000184"}};
if( 'PC' == who ) {
var showlist = '<p style="background-color:#f6f6f6;"><span class="BA-cbox6C">狀態</span><span class="BA-cbox6C">日期</span><span class="BA-cbox6D">平台</span><span>作品名稱</span></p>';
}else{
var showlist = '<p style="background-color:#f6f6f6;"><span class="BA-cbox6C">'+listtitle[who].r3+'</span><span class="BA-cbox6D">'+listtitle[who].r1+'</span><span>作品名稱</span></p>';
}
if( list[who] ){
for(i=0;i<list[who].length;i++) {
showlist += '<p onmouseover="acg_more(\''+who+'\',\''+i+'\')">';
if( undefined !=   list[who][i].type ) {
showlist += '<span class="BA-cbox6C">'+list[who][i].type+'</span>';
}
showlist += '<span class="BA-cbox6C">'+list[who][i].time+'</span><span class="BA-cbox6E">'+list[who][i].machine+'</span><a href="http://acg.gamer.com.tw/acgDetail.php?s='+list[who][i].sn+'" class="IN-acg5">'+list[who][i].title+'</a>';
if( undefined != list[who][i].play ) {
showlist += ' <a title="巴哈帳號直接玩" href="http://ref.gamer.com.tw/redir_play.php?acg_sn='+list[who][i].sn+'" target="_blank"><img src="http://i2.bahamut.com.tw/index_w/Game.gif" border="0"></a>';
}
if( undefined != list[who][i].animeSn ) {
showlist += ' <a href="http://ani.gamer.com.tw/animeRef.php?sn='+list[who][i].animeSn+'" target="_blank" class="BA-freewatch">免費看</a>';
}
if( undefined != list[who][i].gshopcar ){
showlist += ' <a title="看關連商品" href="'+list[who][i].gshopcar+'"><img src="http://i2.bahamut.com.tw/spacer.gif" class="IMG-E46"></a>';
}
showlist += '</p>';
}
}else{
showlist += '<div style="height: 200px; text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; line-height: 200px;">統計中</div>';
}
$('#acg_list').html(showlist);
$('.BA-ctag1now').filter('[id^="acg_"]').attr('className','');
$('#acg_'+who).attr('className','BA-ctag1now');
acg_more(who,0);
if( 'PC' == who ) {
var morelink = '更多：<a href="http://acg.gamer.com.tw/?p=olg">線上遊戲</a><a href="http://acg.gamer.com.tw/?p=web">Web遊戲</a><a href="http://acg.gamer.com.tw/?p=pc">PC 單機</a>';
}else if('TV' == who) {
var morelink = '更多：<a href="http://acg.gamer.com.tw/?p=ps4">PS4</a><a href="http://acg.gamer.com.tw/?p=ps3">PS3</a><a href="http://acg.gamer.com.tw/?p=xbone">XboxOne</a><a href="http://acg.gamer.com.tw/?p=xbox360">Xbox360</a><a href="http://acg.gamer.com.tw/?p=wiiu">WiiU</a><a href="http://acg.gamer.com.tw/?p=psv">PSV</a><a href="http://acg.gamer.com.tw/?p=3ds">3DS</a>';
}else if('AC' == who) {
var morelink = '更多：<a href="http://acg.gamer.com.tw/billboard.php?p=comic&t=8">漫畫</a><a href="http://acg.gamer.com.tw/?p=novel">輕小說</a>';
}else if('QA' == who) {
var morelink = '更多：<a href="http://acg.gamer.com.tw/quarterly.php?d=5">動畫</a>';
}
$('#acg_morelink').html(morelink);
}
function acg_more(who,num) {
var ref = {"PC":{"link":"0000171","more":"0000172"},"TV":{"link":"0000173","more":"0000174"},"AC":{"link":"0000175","more":"0000176"},"QA":{"link":"0000183","more":"0000184"}};
if( undefined != acglist[who][num].pic ) {
$('#acg_pic').get(0).src = acglist[who][num].pic;
}else{
$('#acg_pic').get(0).src = 'http://i2.bahamut.com.tw/acg/noimg120.jpg'
}
$('#acg_pic_link').get(0).href= 'http://acg.gamer.com.tw/acgDetail.php?s='+acglist[who][num].sn;
if( '0' == acglist[who][num].hots ) {
$('#acg_hots').html('人氣：--');
}else{
$('#acg_hots').html('人氣：'+acglist[who][num].hots);
}
}
function acgShowIni(){
var acgBlockAry = ["PC","TV","QA","AC"];
var acgBlockIniKey = Math.floor( Math.random() * acgBlockAry.length );
acgBlockIniKey = (3 <= acgBlockIniKey || 0 >= acgBlockIniKey ) ? 0 : acgBlockIniKey;
acg_change(acgBlockAry[acgBlockIniKey]);
}

/****右邊固定****/
function fBoxRefresh() {
var scrollbarTop = window.pageYOffset || document.documentElement.scrollTop || document.body.scrollTop || 0;
var scrollbarLeft = window.pageXOffset || document.documentElement.scrollLeft|| document.body.scrollLeft || 0;
var contxClientWidth = document.documentElement.clientWidth || document.body.clientWidth || 0;
var contxClientHeight = document.documentElement.clientHeight || document.body.clientHeight || 0;
var fBox_Height = document.getElementById('flyRightBox').offsetHeight;
var fBox_remnants = contxClientHeight - fBox_Height;
if( scrollbarTop > (fBox_Height-contxClientHeight+egg('.BA-center').pos().y) && 0 >= fBox_remnants ){
fBox_style.position = 'fixed';
fBox_style.top = fBox_remnants - 5 + 'px';
fBox_style.left = fBox_posX + 'px';
if( scrollbarLeft ){
fBox_style.left = fBox_posX - scrollbarLeft + 'px';
}
}else if( scrollbarTop > fBox_posY && 0 < fBox_remnants ){
fBox_style.position = 'fixed';
fBox_style.top = '0px';
fBox_style.left = fBox_posX + 'px';
if( scrollbarLeft ){
fBox_style.left = fBox_posX - scrollbarLeft + 'px';
}
}else{
fBox_style.position = '';
}
}
function fBoxResize() {
fBox_style.position = '';
fBox_posX = egg('#flyRightBox').pos().x;
fBoxRefresh();
}
if( document.getElementById('BA-center-id').offsetHeight > document.getElementById('flyRightBox').offsetHeight ){
var fBox_posX = egg('#flyRightBox').pos().x;
var fBox_posY = egg('#flyRightBox').pos().y;
var fBox_style = document.getElementById("flyRightBox").style;
window.onscroll = fBoxRefresh;
window.onresize = fBoxResize;
}

jQuery(".a-mercy-d").click(function() {
var url = this.href;
var goRedirect = false;
var openNew = (this.target) ? true : false;
if( url ) {
jQuery.get( "/ajax/baha_lkasoo.php", { id: jQuery(this).data('ssn') } )
.done(function() {
goRedirect = true;
if( !openNew ){
document.location = url;
}
});
setTimeout(function() {
if (!goRedirect) {
if( !openNew ){
document.location = url;
}
}
}, 1500);
}
if( !openNew ){
return false;
}
});

}
